msg:Staying in the Songyue Room Suite of Beijing Expo Pushen Hotel, the nominal area is 100-150 square meters, which should include the yard area. The indoor area is about 60-70 square meters. Although it is a suite, it can actually be regarded as a single-family villa, with a single door. It is a private courtyard, but there is no bathing pool in the yard. Only the higher-level rooms have them. However, the weather in Beijing is also very cold. There is still a lot of snow in the yard, so if there is a bathing pool, it is probably impossible to take a bath.
.
Two half-moon-shaped screens were made in the yard to increase the depth of field. The fish scale pattern reflected by the evening sunlight through the gaps is still very beautiful. Although it is a high-walled private courtyard, there is plenty of sunlight.
.
The first thing I felt when I entered the room was that it was super warm. I not only turned on the air conditioner and the location early, but also put an electric heater next to the bed. It can be said that it is full of warmth. This is also the hotel where I stayed during this late winter trip to Beijing. The warmest family.
.
Entering the door is a foyer, with side cabinets for easy storage of miscellaneous items. The room key card is made of wood with a ring, which is very beautiful. I collected one when I left the store. Then turn left to the living room. The gabled roof is high and empty, and the left and right are divided into reception areas. In addition to the office area, the desk is quite large, the sofa and coffee table are very unique, especially the coffee table, which is shaped like a cloud, and the large cantilever chandelier is also quite beautiful.
.
The minibar is placed in an antique-style standing cabinet with a bright red paint finish. It has a capsule coffee machine with 2 capsules, 2 bags of customized loose tea, a Chinese tea set, and an electric kettle that boils water very slowly. 4 bottles of Baisui Mountain, the minibar is free but only has 3 bottles of soft drinks. To be honest, for a suite priced at 4,000+ per night, this configuration is definitely too low and not so considerate. The suite is also far from the main building. To order room service, you have to open two doors. It's quite tiring. What's also strange is that there was no welcome fruit plate, but porridge with a very strange combination of raw materials was delivered at night. I could only taste it briefly, but I didn't like it.
.
A corridor from the living room leads to the bedroom. The toilet and cloakroom are on both sides. The courtyard-view toilet has a smart toilet and a mobile phone shelf. It is cute in shape. The cloakroom is extremely small. The only luggage rack is half occupied by a safe, so there is no room to put the suitcases. , unable to understand the design and the significance of the existence of the cloakroom.
.
Compared to the living room, the bedroom is much smaller. The wooden bed frame and completely transparent glass cage shower room look very interesting, so it is not suitable for families with children? All kinds of inconveniences.
.
There is a bedside stool but no sofa by the window. The bathroom space is not spacious. Although there are double basins, they are almost close to each other, which loses the meaning of double basins. The supplies are good, including Parma water and a Dyson hair dryer. Of course, this is also what should be done. Some configurations.
.
The shower room and bathtub are built together, which is a design that I don't like very much, so even though it is a cast iron bathtub from Callandvi, I am not in the mood to take a bath. The shower system feels average.
.
Generally speaking, there are still many unreasonable things in the space design of this suite. In addition to the warm enough temperature, the living experience is not very comfortable. At this price, you can stay at Yihe Aman.

The World Expo is still a bit bleak in this season, and the park staff are still repairing and arranging. There is a beer house in the town. When you walk in, the beer smells good and the quality feels good.
There are some stray dogs in the park, and most of the venues do not have actual exhibition projects. Only the botanical pavilion has exhibition projects.

Children can go to Chibabu Children's Park to play. The area is large and playable, but there is nothing particularly outstanding.

Special mention of this guest room facility.
1. The hardware of the shower room in the guest room is damaged and should be repaired in time;
2. The room is very warm, but very dry, which may be due to the climate in Beijing these days; the ceiling of the room is very high, and it seems that the energy consumption is not low;
3. The sanitation of the courtyard is a problem. There is a lot of dust accumulated in the corners. If conditions permit, it should be washed once a week with a high-pressure water gun

Overall, the hardware of domestic five-star brands is good, but the problem of disrepair is serious. The quality of the service staff of this hotel is relatively high among private brands.

msg:I spent New Year's Eve at the hotel and was satisfied with everything. Maybe it's not the peak time yet, it's very clean and quiet, full of New Year a**osphere.

 Service: I have to give a big thumbs up to the service. All the service staff I met were super service-minded, enthusiastic and motivated, just like their own business. Any excellent service attitude must be a success in management, with top and bottom working together and having consistent interests. This is what business needs to do, and as a customer, I am very excited to see it. From the girls at the front desk, to the young man at the concierge, to the foreman in the restaurant, to the lady who ordered tea, to the shuttle bus driver... we all praised them all.

Aesthetics: The aesthetics of this hotel are so up to par. No wonder even Mercedes-Benz chooses this place for its events. Chinese traditional culture has a big reputation, but it is really empowering to have a hotel that holds traditional cultural projects. Like the tea ceremony and aroma ceremony, there are details in it. From the Chinese knot behind the door, the furnishings in the lobby, flowers and lamps, birds and cages, ginger tea in the public area, paper cups that "unify knowledge and action", and the selection of cultural and creative gifts. . . You can see the professional and delicate thoughts.

Architecture: Rebuilding the General's Mansion a hundred years ago. It's a bit like the Chinese Hall of the Metropolitan Museum of Art in New York - everything is restored using the raw materials of ancient buildings. For details, please refer to the book "This Life in My Hometown" in the room. I like living in ancient buildings very much, just like I lived in Huajiantang Tanhua Mansion in Suzhou. The hotel has charm and style. There are many luxury hotels to choose from in Beijing, but the Anhui-style ancient architecture is unique in Beijing. This is the reason for my choice. From a marketing perspective, this feature is also the biggest differentiation and operating moat of this hotel.

Room: What I am quite satisfied with is that the room has 2 sinks, and the shower and bathtub are also in line with luxury hotel standards. The tea set and incense are very exquisite, and the orchids were chosen very quickly. The view outside the window is wide and the room is spacious; the shortcomings are: it is not a smart toilet, the TV is too small, and it is located diagonally opposite the bed. It is recommended that the hotel change the projection in the future.

Restaurant: The service attitude is excellent. The presentation is also beautiful, and there is a pot of my favorite pink rhododendron on the dining table. We had three meals in the restaurant. Lunch order-Huaiyang cuisine; dinner buffet with stove; breakfast buffet. However, I can only say that it is not a matter of attitude, but probably a matter of the level of the chef, or maybe there are restrictions on cooking fumes in the expo? It was really exhausting to eat.

 Things to do: I think the lanterns are pretty good to watch, but it‚Äôs too cold and they freeze back. You can go up to Yongning Tower to enjoy the breeze; the CITIC Bookstore on the top floor of the Botanical Garden is not interesting, but the wooden giraffe on the platform outside the bookstore is very artistic and worth checking in.

Just sauce. All in all, I was happy, except that Beijing was too cold. . . .

msg:Affected by the epidemic, I have always wanted to take my parents on a leisure vacation but failed. Today, I found the Pushen Hotel located at the Yanqing World Horticultural Exposition on the Internet, so I called the front desk to inquire about the check-in situation.
After an hour's drive, I soon arrived at the hotel surrounded by green trees and mountains, where blue sky and white clouds, green grass, scattered flowers are in full bloom, and in the clumps of reeds, groups of wild ducks sing cheerfully on the quiet water. Singing, the beautiful Huizhou-style courtyards make people feel relaxed and happy. The front desk staff Xiao Gao and Nan Nan received us very warmly and caringly, and they introduced me in detail. Originally booked a king bed and a Songyue suite, we were upgraded to two suites. The waiter warmly helped us carry our luggage, took us through the quiet and winding road, and walked into the small courtyard. The grand decoration style, the antique furnishings, the large hot spring pool, the soft and comfortable big bed... The service staff Yuan Zhuying is very conscientious, helping my parents to solve their problems, and enthusiastically introducing them to the surrounding attractions. My parents are very satisfied.
After settling down, I took my mother to do a relaxing massage with essential oils. The professional technique of masseuse Xiaohong made my mother full of praise. Xiaohong taught my mother which acupoints to treat migraine headaches, which acupoints to treat cervical discomfort, and how to massage for gray hair. ...Mother is very happy to say that she has learned health care knowledge from Teacher Xiaohong.
The hotel arranged a battery car to pick us up for a visit to the Expo. In the hot weather, it is really pleasant to take a car to enjoy the scenery.
The shopping activities in the China Duty Free Store are very good. There are many dazzling products for us to choose from. It is really a perfect combination of tourism and shopping.
The restaurant is clean and tidy, with a wide variety of food, very rich and delicious, and the dining environment is very good.
On the top of the hill to the east of the small courtyard, the majestic building, we sat under the big names with good weather and clear river, and had a bird's-eye view of the beautiful surroundings and the cool breeze. We really felt that our trip was worthwhile.

msg:The hardware of the hotel is excellent, but the service is such a mess that it shatters to the floor. The hotel is on the north side of the Expo Park. Visitors to the Expo usually enter through Gate 1 on the south side. The activities on the north side are mostly hotel guests, which are very quiet. Next to the Gui River, the scenery is excellent, and it is very comfortable to lay a floor mat by the river to enjoy the river view.
